if (!is_file('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md') != '4b4d9f5c0df2250eecf432cead0f797caf44965c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md') !== '4b4d9f5c0df2250eecf432cead0f797caf44965c') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md') !== '61a5f189d0d3b240f37ec64f467cb713291f4fab') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md') !== '4b4d9f5c0df2250eecf432cead0f797caf44965c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/oidplus_custom_guid.md');
		}
	}
}

	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') != '6d9bf7185faf92981dcb20486ebe0426fd1e02ae') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '6d9bf7185faf92981dcb20486ebe0426fd1e02ae') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '1d7c2d600146a8036bbcd347b0d374ed6a68841e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '6d9bf7185faf92981dcb20486ebe0426fd1e02ae') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '85f329c953a057d6e057469adf821478a34c5f99') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '85f329c953a057d6e057469adf821478a34c5f99') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '0251596863995b54b1edac930d4a678fa7454e6d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '85f329c953a057d6e057469adf821478a34c5f99') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 1333\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 1333') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
